```typescript
//   title: string;
//   version: string;
// }

// ‚ùå Type - KH√îNG TH·ªÇ redeclare
type Window = { title: string; };
// type Window = { version: string; }; // Error: Duplicate identifier
```

**2. Union Types (Type ONLY):**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ Type - C√≥ th·ªÉ define union types
type Status = 'loading' | 'success' | 'error';
type StringOrNumber = string | number;
type ApiResponse = SuccessResponse | ErrorResponse;

// ‚ùå Interface - Kh√¥ng th·ªÉ define unions tr·ª±c ti·∫øp
// interface Status = 'loading' | 'success' | 'error'; // Syntax error
```

**3. Computed Properties (Type BETTER):**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ Type - Full support cho computed properties
type EventMap = {
  [K in 'click' | 'hover' | 'focus']: (event: Event) => void;
};

type DynamicObject<T> = {
  [K in keyof T]: T[K][];
};

// ‚ö†Ô∏è Interface - Limited support
interface EventMap {
  // Ph·∫£i vi·∫øt manual
  click: (event: Event) => void;
  hover: (event: Event) => void;
  focus: (event: Event) => void;
}
```

**4. Extending vs Intersection:**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ Interface extending
interface Animal {
  name: string;
}

interface Dog extends Animal {
  breed: string;
}

// ‚úÖ Type intersection
type Animal = {
  name: string;
};

type Dog = Animal & {
  breed: string;
};

// üéØ C·∫£ hai ƒë·ªÅu work t∆∞∆°ng t·ª± cho simple cases
```

#### **üöÄ ADVANCED USE CASES:**

**Interface cho OOP patterns:**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ Interface - Perfect cho classes v√† inheritance
interface Drawable {
  draw(): void;
}

interface Resizable {
  resize(width: number, height: number): void;
}

// Multiple interface implementation
class Shape implements Drawable, Resizable {
  draw() { /* implementation */ }
  resize(width: number, height: number) { /* implementation */ }
}

// ‚úÖ Declaration merging cho library augmentation
declare global {
  interface Array<T> {
    myCustomMethod(): T[];
  }
}
```

**Type cho functional programming:**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ Type - Perfect cho utility types v√† transformations
type Partial<T> = {
  [P in keyof T]?: T[P];
};

type ApiEndpoint<T> = {
  url: string;
  method: 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'DELETE';
  body?: T;
  response: Promise<T>;
};

// Conditional types
type NonNullable<T> = T extends null | undefined ? never : T;

// Complex mappings
type EventHandlers<T> = {
  [K in keyof T as `on${Capitalize<string & K>}`]: (value: T[K]) => void;
};
```

#### **üéØ BEST PRACTICES - KHI N√ÄO D√ôNG G√å:**

**‚úÖ S·ª≠ d·ª•ng `interface` khi:**
```typescript
// 1. Define object shapes cho classes
interface UserService {
  getUser(id: number): Promise<User>;
  updateUser(id: number, data: Partial<User>): Promise<User>;
}

class ApiUserService implements UserService {
  // Implementation
}

// 2. Public API definitions (libraries)
interface ComponentProps {
  children?: React.ReactNode;
  className?: string;
}

// 3. C√≥ th·ªÉ c·∫ßn extend sau n√†y
interface BaseConfig {
  apiUrl: string;
}

interface ProductionConfig extends BaseConfig {
  ssl: true;
}

// 4. Library augmentation
declare module 'react' {
  interface CSSProperties {
    '--custom-property'?: string;
  }
}
```

**‚úÖ S·ª≠ d·ª•ng `type` khi:**
```typescript
// 1. Union types
type Theme = 'light' | 'dark' | 'auto';
type HttpMethod = 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'DELETE';

// 2. Complex type transformations
type EventMap<T> = {
  [K in keyof T]: (data: T[K]) => void;
};

// 3. Computed property names
type ApiRoutes = {
  [K in 'users' | 'posts' | 'comments' as `api/${K}`]: string;
};

// 4. Conditional logic
type NonEmptyArray<T> = [T, ...T[]];

// 5. Primitive type aliases
type ID = string | number;
type Timestamp = number;
```

#### **üî• MODERN RECOMMENDATIONS:**

```typescript
// üéØ HYBRID APPROACH - Use both strategically!

// ‚úÖ interface cho object shapes
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

// ‚úÖ type cho unions v√† utilities
type UserStatus = 'active' | 'inactive' | 'banned';
type UserWithStatus = User & { status: UserStatus };

// ‚úÖ interface cho component props
interface ButtonProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  onClick: () => void;
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary';
}

// ‚úÖ type cho complex derived types
type ButtonEvents = {
  [K in keyof ButtonProps as K extends `on${string}` ? K : never]: ButtonProps[K];
};
```

**üí° GHI NH·ªö:**
- **`interface`** = OOP style, extensible, declaration merging üèóÔ∏è
- **`type`** = Functional style, unions, computed properties üéØ

**Choose based on your use case, team style, v√† TypeScript version!** üöÄ

---

### TS4: Browser c√≥ th·ªÉ ch·∫°y TypeScript kh√¥ng? T·∫°i sao?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

**‚ùå KH√îNG!** Browser **KH√îNG TH·ªÇ** ch·∫°y TypeScript tr·ª±c ti·∫øp. ƒê√¢y l√† m·ªôt **FUNDAMENTAL CONCEPT** c·∫ßn hi·ªÉu r√µ.

#### **üî• T·∫†I SAO Browser KH√îNG ch·∫°y ƒë∆∞·ª£c TypeScript:**

**1. TypeScript IS NOT JavaScript:**
```typescript
// ‚ùå Code n√†y browser KH√îNG hi·ªÉu
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
}

function greetUser(user: User): string {
  return `Hello, ${user.name}!`;
}

// Browser s·∫Ω throw: SyntaxError: Unexpected token ':'
```

**2. Browsers ch·ªâ hi·ªÉu JavaScript (ES5/ES6+):**
```javascript
// ‚úÖ Code n√†y browser HI·ªÇU ƒë∆∞·ª£c
function greetUser(user) {
  return `Hello, ${user.name}!`;
}
```

#### **üîÑ QUY TR√åNH COMPILATION:**

```
üìù TypeScript (.ts)
        ‚Üì
    üîß TypeScript Compiler (tsc)
        ‚Üì
üì¶ JavaScript (.js)
        ‚Üì
    üåê Browser Engine
        ‚Üì
    üöÄ Execution
```

#### **üõ†Ô∏è C√ÅC C√ÅCH TRANSFORM TypeScript:**

**1. TypeScript Compiler (tsc):**
```bash
# C√†i ƒë·∫∑t TypeScript compiler
npm install -g typescript

# Compile single file
tsc app.ts

# Compile entire project
tsc --project tsconfig.json
```

**Example compilation:**
```typescript
// Input: app.ts
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
}

const user: User = {
  id: 1,
  name: 'John'
};

function greetUser(user: User): string {
  return `Hello, ${user.name}!`;
}
```

```javascript
// Output: app.js (compiled)
"use strict";

const user = {
  id: 1,
  name: 'John'
};

function greetUser(user) {
  return `Hello, ${user.name}!`;
}
```

**2. Build Tools Integration:**

**Webpack v·ªõi TypeScript:**
```javascript
// webpack.config.js
module.exports = {
  entry: './src/index.ts',
  module: {
    rules: [
      {
        test: /\.ts$/,
        use: 'ts-loader',
        exclude: /node_modules/
      }
    ]
  },
  resolve: {
    extensions: ['.ts', '.js']
  }
};
```

**Vite v·ªõi TypeScript (Modern):**
```javascript
// vite.config.ts - ZERO CONFIG!
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';

export default defineConfig({
  // Vite t·ª± ƒë·ªông handle .ts files
});
```

**3. Real-time Development:**

**Babel-TypeScript:**
```json
// .babelrc
{
  "presets": [
    "@babel/preset-env",
    "@babel/preset-typescript"
  ]
}
```

**ts-node (Development only):**
```bash
# Ch·∫°y TypeScript tr·ª±c ti·∫øp (development)
npx ts-node src/app.ts

# Nh∆∞ng v·∫´n c·∫ßn compile cho production!
```

#### **üöÄ MODERN WORKFLOW:**

**Development:**
```typescript
// üìù Write TypeScript
const users: User[] = await fetchUsers();

// üîÑ Hot reload v·ªõi type checking
// Tools: Vite, Webpack Dev Server, ts-node
```

**Production Build:**
```bash
# üîß Build process
npm run build

# Output: Optimized JavaScript bundles
# dist/
#   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.js (compiled + minified)
#   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ vendor.js (dependencies)
#   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ style.css
```

#### **‚ö° WHAT HAPPENS TO TypeScript FEATURES:**

**Type Annotations ‚Üí REMOVED:**
```typescript
// TypeScript
function calculate(a: number, b: number): number {
  return a + b;
}

// Compiled JavaScript
function calculate(a, b) {
  return a + b;
}
```

**Interfaces ‚Üí DISAPPEAR:**
```typescript
// TypeScript
interface Config {
  apiUrl: string;
  timeout: number;
}

// Compiled JavaScript
// (interfaces ho√†n to√†n bi·∫øn m·∫•t!)
```

**Enums ‚Üí BECOME Objects:**
```typescript
// TypeScript
enum Status {
  PENDING = 'pending',
  APPROVED = 'approved'
}

// Compiled JavaScript
var Status;
(function (Status) {
  Status["PENDING"] = "pending";
  Status["APPROVED"] = "approved";
})(Status || (Status = {}));
```

**Generics ‚Üí ERASED:**
```typescript
// TypeScript
function identity<T>(arg: T): T {
  return arg;
}

// Compiled JavaScript
function identity(arg) {
  return arg;
}
```

#### **üîç HOW TO VERIFY:**

**1. Browser DevTools:**
```javascript
// Open browser console v√† th·ª≠:
const user: User = { id: 1, name: 'John' };
// SyntaxError: Unexpected token ':'
```

**2. HTML Script Tag:**
```html
<!-- ‚ùå ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y S·∫º L·ªñI -->
<script src="app.ts"></script>

<!-- ‚úÖ ƒêi·ªÅu n√†y WORK -->
<script src="app.js"></script>
```

**3. Online TypeScript Playground:**
Visit [typescriptlang.org/play](https://typescriptlang.org/play) ƒë·ªÉ see compilation process!

#### **üí° KEY TAKEAWAYS:**

```
üîπ TypeScript = DEVELOPMENT TIME tool
üîπ JavaScript = RUNTIME language
üîπ Compilation = MANDATORY step
üîπ Type safety = COMPILE TIME only
üîπ Browser = JavaScript ONLY environment
```

**üéØ INTERVIEW TIP:**
Always emphasize r·∫±ng TypeScript **MUST BE COMPILED** to JavaScript tr∆∞·ªõc khi browser c√≥ th·ªÉ run. ƒê√¢y l√† **fundamental difference** gi·ªØa development v√† production environments!

**GHI NH·ªö:** TypeScript in browser = **JavaScript with extra steps!** üîÑ

---

### TS5: Type Narrowing trong TypeScript - C√°ch ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

Type Narrowing l√† **CORE CONCEPT** trong TypeScript ƒë·ªÉ **THU H·∫∏P TYPE** t·ª´ union type th√†nh specific type. ƒê√¢y l√† **ADVANCED TECHNIQUE** gi√∫p TypeScript hi·ªÉu ch√≠nh x√°c type trong runtime.

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL CONCEPT:**

**Type Narrowing = T·ª´ WIDE TYPE ‚Üí NARROW TYPE**

```typescript
// üåê WIDE TYPE (Union)
type StringOrNumber = string | number;

function processValue(value: StringOrNumber) {
  // üîç NARROWING: Thu h·∫πp type ƒë·ªÉ TypeScript hi·ªÉu r√µ
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript bi·∫øt: value is STRING
    return value.toUpperCase(); // ‚úÖ String methods available
  } else {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript bi·∫øt: value is NUMBER
    return value.toFixed(2); // ‚úÖ Number methods available
  }
}
```

#### **üõ†Ô∏è C√ÅC PH∆Ø∆†NG PH√ÅP TYPE NARROWING:**

**1. typeof Guards:**
```typescript
function handleInput(input: string | number | boolean) {
  if (typeof input === "string") {
    console.log(`String: ${input.length} characters`); // ‚úÖ string methods
  } else if (typeof input === "number") {
    console.log(`Number: ${input.toFixed(2)}`); // ‚úÖ number methods
  } else {
    console.log(`Boolean: ${input ? "true" : "false"}`); // ‚úÖ boolean context
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: typeof returns "string" | "number" | "boolean" | "object" | "undefined" | "function"
```

**2. instanceof Guards:**
```typescript
class Dog {
  bark() { return "Woof!"; }
}

class Cat {
  meow() { return "Meow!"; }
}

function makeSound(animal: Dog | Cat) {
  if (animal instanceof Dog) {
    return animal.bark(); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's Dog
  } else {
    return animal.meow(); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's Cat
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: instanceof ki·ªÉm tra prototype chain
```

**3. in Operator (Property Check):**
```typescript
interface Bird {
  fly(): void;
  feathers: number;
}

interface Fish {
  swim(): void;
  scales: number;
}

function move(animal: Bird | Fish) {
  if ("fly" in animal) {
    animal.fly(); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's Bird
    console.log(`Bird has ${animal.feathers} feathers`);
  } else {
    animal.swim(); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's Fish
    console.log(`Fish has ${animal.scales} scales`);
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: "property" in object ki·ªÉm tra property existence
```

**4. Literal Type Guards:**
```typescript
type Status = "loading" | "success" | "error";

function handleStatus(status: Status) {
  if (status === "loading") {
    return "ƒêang t·∫£i..."; // ‚úÖ Exact literal type
  } else if (status === "success") {
    return "Th√†nh c√¥ng!"; // ‚úÖ Exact literal type
  } else {
    return "C√≥ l·ªói x·∫£y ra!"; // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's "error"
  }
}
```

**5. Custom Type Guards (Advanced):**
```typescript
// üéØ CUSTOM TYPE PREDICATE FUNCTIONS
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

interface Admin {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  permissions: string[];
}

// üîß Custom Type Guard Function
function isAdmin(user: User | Admin): user is Admin {
  return 'permissions' in user; // Return type: user is Admin
}

function handleUser(user: User | Admin) {
  if (isAdmin(user)) {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows user is Admin
    console.log(`Admin ${user.name} has ${user.permissions.length} permissions`);
  } else {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows user is User
    console.log(`User ${user.name} email: ${user.email}`);
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: "x is Type" syntax l√† Type Predicate
```

#### **‚ö° ADVANCED NARROWING PATTERNS:**

**1. Discriminated Unions:**
```typescript
// üè∑Ô∏è TAGGED UNION v·ªõi common property
interface LoadingState {
  status: "loading"; // üè∑Ô∏è Discriminator property
}

interface SuccessState {
  status: "success"; // üè∑Ô∏è Discriminator property
  data: any[];
}

interface ErrorState {
  status: "error"; // üè∑Ô∏è Discriminator property
  message: string;
}

type AppState = LoadingState | SuccessState | ErrorState;

function renderState(state: AppState) {
  // üéØ PERFECT NARROWING b·∫±ng discriminator
  switch (state.status) {
    case "loading":
      return <div>Loading...</div>; // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows LoadingState
    case "success":
      return <div>{state.data.length} items</div>; // ‚úÖ data property available
    case "error":
      return <div>Error: {state.message}</div>; // ‚úÖ message property available
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Discriminated Union = Union + Common Property v·ªõi literal types
```

**2. Exhaustiveness Checking:**
```typescript
type Theme = "light" | "dark" | "auto";

function getThemeColor(theme: Theme): string {
  switch (theme) {
    case "light":
      return "#ffffff";
    case "dark":
      return "#000000";
    case "auto":
      return "#f0f0f0";
    default:
      // üö® EXHAUSTIVENESS CHECK
      const exhaustiveCheck: never = theme;
      throw new Error(`Unhandled theme: ${exhaustiveCheck}`);
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: never type gi√∫p catch missing cases khi th√™m new literal types
```

**3. Nullish Narrowing:**
```typescript
function processName(name: string | null | undefined) {
  // ‚ùå UNSAFE - might be null/undefined
  // return name.toUpperCase();

  // ‚úÖ SAFE - narrowing first
  if (name != null) { // Removes both null AND undefined
    return name.toUpperCase(); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows name is string
  }
  return "Unknown";
}

// Alternative v·ªõi Optional Chaining
function processNameSafe(name: string | null | undefined) {
  return name?.toUpperCase() ?? "Unknown";
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: name != null removes both null AND undefined
// üìù GHI NH·ªû: name !== null ch·ªâ removes null, NOT undefined
```

#### **üéØ PRACTICAL EXAMPLES:**

**Real-world API Response Handling:**
```typescript
interface ApiResponse<T> {
  success: boolean;
  data?: T;
  error?: string;
}

function handleApiResponse<T>(response: ApiResponse<T>) {
  if (response.success && response.data) {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows data exists v√† success = true
    return response.data; // ‚úÖ Type T available
  } else if (!response.success && response.error) {
    // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows error exists v√† success = false
    throw new Error(response.error); // ‚úÖ string methods available
  } else {
    throw new Error("Invalid API response format");
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªû: Multiple conditions for comprehensive narrowing
```

**React Props Narrowing:**
```typescript
interface ButtonProps {
  variant: "primary" | "secondary";
  size: "small" | "medium" | "large";
  disabled?: boolean;
  onClick?: () => void;
}

function Button({ variant, size, disabled, onClick }: ButtonProps) {
  // üéØ NARROWING cho conditional rendering
  if (disabled) {
    return (
      <button className={`btn-${variant} btn-${size} btn-disabled`}>
        {/* ‚úÖ TypeScript knows disabled is true */}
        Disabled Button
      </button>
    );
  }

  return (
    <button
      className={`btn-${variant} btn-${size}`}
      onClick={onClick} // ‚úÖ Safe to use
    >
      Active Button
    </button>
  );
}
```

#### **üí° INTERVIEW INSIGHTS:**

**üîπ KHI N√ÄO S·ª¨ D·ª§NG:**
- Union types c·∫ßn specific handling
- API responses v·ªõi multiple states
- Event handling v·ªõi different event types
- Form validation v·ªõi conditional logic

**üîπ COMMON MISTAKES:**
```typescript
// ‚ùå SAI: Kh√¥ng narrow type
function badExample(value: string | number) {
  return value.toUpperCase(); // üí• Error: toUpperCase not exist on number
}

// ‚úÖ ƒê√öNG: Narrow type first
function goodExample(value: string | number) {
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    return value.toUpperCase(); // ‚úÖ Works
  }
  return value.toString().toUpperCase();
}
```

**üîπ PERFORMANCE IMPACT:**
- Type narrowing = **COMPILE TIME** only
- **NO RUNTIME OVERHEAD**
- Improves **DEVELOPMENT EXPERIENCE** v√† **TYPE SAFETY**

#### **üöÄ TYPE NARROWING WORKFLOW:**

```
üåê Wide Union Type
        ‚Üì
üîç Runtime Check (typeof, instanceof, in, custom guard)
        ‚Üì
üéØ Narrowed Specific Type
        ‚Üì
‚úÖ Safe Property/Method Access
```

**üìù GOLDEN RULES:**
1. **Always narrow BEFORE access** union type properties
2. **Use type guards** cho complex narrowing logic
3. **Discriminated unions** cho state management
4. **Custom type predicates** cho reusable logic
5. **Exhaustiveness checking** v·ªõi never type

**GHI NH·ªû:** Type Narrowing = **TypeScript's way of making UNSAFE code SAFE!** üõ°Ô∏è

---

### TS6: `unknown` vs `any` - S·ª± kh√°c bi·ªát v√† khi n√†o s·ª≠ d·ª•ng?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

ƒê√¢y l√† **CRUCIAL DISTINCTION** trong TypeScript! `unknown` v√† `any` ƒë·ªÅu represent "anything", nh∆∞ng **SAFETY LEVEL** ho√†n to√†n kh√°c nhau.

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL DIFFERENCE:**

| Aspect | **`any`** | **`unknown`** |
|--------|-----------|---------------|
| **Type Safety** | ‚ùå **UNSAFE** | ‚úÖ **SAFE** |
| **Type Checking** | **DISABLED** | **ENABLED** |
| **Direct Access** | ‚úÖ **Allowed** | ‚ùå **Forbidden** |
| **Need Type Guards** | ‚ùå **No** | ‚úÖ **Required** |
| **Best Practice** | üö´ **Avoid** | ‚úÖ **Preferred** |

#### **üõ†Ô∏è `any` - THE ESCAPE HATCH:**

```typescript
let value: any = 42;

// ‚ùå DANGEROUS: No type checking whatsoever!
value.foo.bar.baz; // üí• Runtime error, TypeScript won't catch
value(); // üí• Runtime error if not a function
value[0][1][2]; // üí• Runtime error if not nested array
value.toUpperCase(); // üí• Runtime error if not string

// üò± TYPESCRIPT GIVES UP: No intellisense, no safety!
```

**ANY = "Trust me, I know what I'm doing" (but usually you don't!) üö´**

#### **üõ°Ô∏è `unknown` - THE SAFE ALTERNATIVE:**

```typescript
let value: unknown = 42;

// ‚úÖ SAFE: TypeScript forces type checking!
// value.foo; // ‚ùå Compile error: Object is of type 'unknown'
// value(); // ‚ùå Compile error: Cannot invoke unknown type
// value.toUpperCase(); // ‚ùå Compile error: Property doesn't exist

// ‚úÖ MUST USE TYPE GUARDS first:
if (typeof value === "string") {
  console.log(value.toUpperCase()); // ‚úÖ Now it's safe!
}

if (typeof value === "number") {
  console.log(value.toFixed(2)); // ‚úÖ Number methods available
}
```

**UNKNOWN = "I don't know what this is, let me check first!" ‚úÖ**

#### **üìä DETAILED COMPARISON:**

**1. Assignment TO them:**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ BOTH accept anything
let anyValue: any = "hello";
let unknownValue: unknown = "hello";

anyValue = 42; // ‚úÖ OK
unknownValue = 42; // ‚úÖ OK

anyValue = { name: "John" }; // ‚úÖ OK
unknownValue = { name: "John" }; // ‚úÖ OK

anyValue = [1, 2, 3]; // ‚úÖ OK
unknownValue = [1, 2, 3]; // ‚úÖ OK
```

**2. Assignment FROM them:**
```typescript
let anyValue: any = "hello";
let unknownValue: unknown = "hello";

// ‚ùå ANY: Can assign to ANYTHING (dangerous!)
let str1: string = anyValue; // ‚úÖ No error (but dangerous!)
let num1: number = anyValue; // ‚úÖ No error (but dangerous!)
let bool1: boolean = anyValue; // ‚úÖ No error (but dangerous!)

// ‚úÖ UNKNOWN: Cannot assign without type checking
// let str2: string = unknownValue; // ‚ùå Error: Type 'unknown' not assignable
// let num2: number = unknownValue; // ‚ùå Error

// ‚úÖ MUST narrow type first
if (typeof unknownValue === "string") {
  let str2: string = unknownValue; // ‚úÖ Now it's safe!
}
```

**3. Property Access:**
```typescript
let anyValue: any = { name: "John", age: 30 };
let unknownValue: unknown = { name: "John", age: 30 };

// ‚ùå ANY: Direct access (unsafe)
console.log(anyValue.name); // ‚úÖ No error (but risky)
console.log(anyValue.nonexistent); // ‚úÖ No error (returns undefined)

// ‚úÖ UNKNOWN: Must check first
// console.log(unknownValue.name); // ‚ùå Error

// ‚úÖ Safe way with type guards
if (unknownValue && typeof unknownValue === "object" && "name" in unknownValue) {
  console.log((unknownValue as { name: string }).name); // ‚úÖ Safe
}
```

#### **üéØ PRACTICAL USE CASES:**

**1. API Responses (Best Practice with `unknown`):**
```typescript
// ‚ùå BAD: Using any
async function fetchUserBad(): Promise<any> {
  const response = await fetch('/api/user');
  const data = await response.json(); // Returns any
  return data; // ‚ùå No type safety
}

// ‚úÖ GOOD: Using unknown
async function fetchUserGood(): Promise<unknown> {
  const response = await fetch('/api/user');
  const data = await response.json(); // Returns any, but we convert to unknown
  return data; // ‚úÖ Forces type checking at usage
}

// Usage
async function handleUser() {
  const userData = await fetchUserGood();

  // ‚úÖ Must validate first
  if (isUser(userData)) {
    console.log(`User: ${userData.name}`); // ‚úÖ Type-safe
  }
}

// üîß Type guard function
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

function isUser(obj: unknown): obj is User {
  return (
    obj !== null &&
    typeof obj === "object" &&
    typeof (obj as User).id === "number" &&
    typeof (obj as User).name === "string" &&
    typeof (obj as User).email === "string"
  );
}
```

**2. Error Handling:**
```typescript
// ‚ùå BAD: Using any
function handleErrorBad(error: any) {
  console.log(error.message); // üí• Might crash if error has no message
  throw error; // ‚ùå No type safety
}

// ‚úÖ GOOD: Using unknown
function handleErrorGood(error: unknown) {
  // ‚úÖ Safe error handling
  if (error instanceof Error) {
    console.log(error.message); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's Error
    console.log(error.stack);
  } else if (typeof error === "string") {
    console.log(error); // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows it's string
  } else {
    console.log("Unknown error occurred"); // ‚úÖ Fallback
  }
}

// Better: Custom error type guard
function isErrorWithMessage(error: unknown): error is { message: string } {
  return (
    typeof error === "object" &&
    error !== null &&
    "message" in error &&
    typeof (error as { message: unknown }).message === "string"
  );
}

function safeErrorHandler(error: unknown) {
  if (isErrorWithMessage(error)) {
    console.log(error.message); // ‚úÖ Safe access
  } else {
    console.log("Error without message");
  }
}
```

**3. JSON Parsing:**
```typescript
// ‚ùå BAD: JSON.parse returns any
function parseJsonBad(jsonString: string) {
  const data = JSON.parse(jsonString); // any type
  return data.user.name; // üí• Might crash
}

// ‚úÖ GOOD: Treat as unknown and validate
function parseJsonGood(jsonString: string) {
  const data: unknown = JSON.parse(jsonString);

  // ‚úÖ Validate structure first
  if (isValidUserData(data)) {
    return data.user.name; // ‚úÖ Type-safe
  }

  throw new Error("Invalid JSON structure");
}

function isValidUserData(data: unknown): data is { user: { name: string } } {
  return (
    data !== null &&
    typeof data === "object" &&
    "user" in data &&
    typeof (data as any).user === "object" &&
    typeof (data as any).user.name === "string"
  );
}
```

**4. Library Migration:**
```typescript
// üîÑ MIGRATION STRATEGY: any ‚Üí unknown
// Step 1: Change return type from any to unknown
function oldLibraryCall(): unknown { // Was: any
  return legacyLibrary.getData();
}

// Step 2: Add type guards where needed
function useLibraryData() {
  const data = oldLibraryCall();

  // Must add validation now
  if (isExpectedFormat(data)) {
    processData(data); // ‚úÖ Type-safe
  }
}
```

#### **‚ö° ADVANCED PATTERNS:**

**1. Generic Functions with unknown:**
```typescript
// ‚úÖ SAFE generic function
function safeCast<T>(value: unknown, validator: (val: unknown) => val is T): T | null {
  return validator(value) ? value : null;
}

// Usage
const userData = safeCast(apiResponse, isUser);
if (userData) {
  console.log(userData.name); // ‚úÖ Typed as User
}
```

**2. Unknown in Union Types:**
```typescript
type SafeApiResponse =
  | { success: true; data: unknown } // ‚úÖ Unknown forces validation
  | { success: false; error: string };

function handleResponse(response: SafeApiResponse) {
  if (response.success) {
    // Must validate response.data before use
    if (isUser(response.data)) {
      console.log(response.data.name); // ‚úÖ Safe
    }
  } else {
    console.log(response.error); // ‚úÖ Already typed as string
  }
}
```

#### **üö® MIGRATION GUIDE: `any` ‚Üí `unknown`:**

```typescript
// üîÑ STEP-BY-STEP MIGRATION

// Before (unsafe):
function processData(data: any) {
  return data.items.map((item: any) => item.name.toUpperCase());
}

// After (safe):
function processDataSafe(data: unknown) {
  // Add validation
  if (isDataWithItems(data)) {
    return data.items
      .filter(isItemWithName) // Filter valid items
      .map(item => item.name.toUpperCase()); // ‚úÖ Safe
  }
  throw new Error("Invalid data format");
}

// Type guards needed:
function isDataWithItems(data: unknown): data is { items: unknown[] } {
  return (
    data !== null &&
    typeof data === "object" &&
    "items" in data &&
    Array.isArray((data as any).items)
  );
}

function isItemWithName(item: unknown): item is { name: string } {
  return (
    item !== null &&
    typeof item === "object" &&
    "name" in item &&
    typeof (item as any).name === "string"
  );
}
```

#### **üí° INTERVIEW INSIGHTS:**

**üîπ KHI N√ÄO S·ª¨ D·ª§NG `any`:**
- üò§ **NEVER** in new code! (n·∫øu c√≥ th·ªÉ)
- üîÑ **Legacy code migration** (temporary)
- üì¶ **Third-party libraries** without types (use `@types` if available)
- ‚ö° **Rapid prototyping** (but refactor later!)

**üîπ KHI N√ÄO S·ª¨ D·ª§NG `unknown`:**
- ‚úÖ **API responses** ch∆∞a bi·∫øt structure
- ‚úÖ **Error handling** generic errors
- ‚úÖ **JSON parsing** external data
- ‚úÖ **User input** validation
- ‚úÖ **Library functions** returning uncertain types

**üîπ PERFORMANCE:**
- Both `any` v√† `unknown` = **NO RUNTIME COST**
- Difference = **COMPILE TIME** type checking only
- `unknown` = **Better developer experience** + **Fewer runtime errors**

#### **üéØ DECISION FRAMEWORK:**

```
‚ùì Do you know the exact type?
   ‚îú‚îÄ Yes ‚Üí Use specific type
   ‚îî‚îÄ No ‚Üì

‚ùì Can you validate the type?
   ‚îú‚îÄ Yes ‚Üí Use unknown + type guards
   ‚îî‚îÄ No ‚Üì

‚ùì Is this legacy/migration code?
   ‚îú‚îÄ Yes ‚Üí Use any (temporarily)
   ‚îî‚îÄ No ‚Üí Refactor to use unknown
```

**üìù GOLDEN RULES:**
1. **Default to `unknown`** when uncertain about types
2. **Avoid `any`** unless absolutely necessary
3. **Always validate `unknown`** before usage
4. **Create type guards** for common validation patterns
5. **Migrate `any` to `unknown`** in existing code

**GHI NH·ªö:**
- `any` = **"I don't care about types"** üö´
- `unknown` = **"I care about types, let me check first"** ‚úÖ

**INTERVIEW TIP:** Always emphasize r·∫±ng `unknown` is **TYPE-SAFE** alternative to `any`, v√† showcase your knowledge c·ªßa proper type validation patterns! üéØ

---

### TS7: Decorator trong TypeScript - Kh√°i ni·ªám v√† ·ª©ng d·ª•ng?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

Decorators l√† **EXPERIMENTAL FEATURE** trong TypeScript cho ph√©p **MODIFY BEHAVIOR** c·ªßa classes, methods, properties, v√† parameters th√¥ng qua **METADATA v√† RUNTIME MANIPULATION**.

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL CONCEPT:**

**Decorator = Function that MODIFIES another function/class**

```typescript
// üè∑Ô∏è BASIC DECORATOR SYNTAX
@decoratorFunction
class MyClass {
  @propertyDecorator
  property: string;

  @methodDecorator
  method() {}
}

// Equivalent to:
MyClass = decoratorFunction(MyClass);
```

#### **‚öôÔ∏è ENABLING DECORATORS:**

**tsconfig.json:**
```json
{
  "compilerOptions": {
    "experimentalDecorators": true,    // ‚úÖ Enable legacy decorators
    "emitDecoratorMetadata": true      // ‚úÖ Emit metadata (cho reflection)
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Decorators v·∫´n l√† EXPERIMENTAL feature!
```

#### **üõ†Ô∏è TYPES OF DECORATORS:**

**1. Class Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ CLASS DECORATOR FUNCTION
function Component(config: { selector: string; template: string }) {
  return function<T extends { new(...args: any[]): {} }>(constructor: T) {
    return class extends constructor {
      selector = config.selector;
      template = config.template;

      // ‚úÖ Add new functionality to class
      render() {
        console.log(`Rendering ${this.selector}: ${this.template}`);
      }
    };
  };
}

// üè∑Ô∏è USAGE
@Component({
  selector: 'app-user',
  template: '<div>User Component</div>'
})
class UserComponent {
  name = 'John';
}

// Test
const user = new UserComponent() as any;
user.render(); // "Rendering app-user: <div>User Component</div>"

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Class decorator receives constructor function
```

**2. Method Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ METHOD DECORATOR for performance tracking
function benchmark(target: any, propertyName: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
  const method = descriptor.value;

  descriptor.value = function (...args: any[]) {
    console.time(`${propertyName} execution time`);
    const result = method.apply(this, args);
    console.timeEnd(`${propertyName} execution time`);
    return result;
  };
}

class DataProcessor {
  @benchmark
  processLargeDataset(data: any[]) {
    // Simulate heavy computation
    return data.map(item => item * 2);
  }
}

// Usage
const processor = new DataProcessor();
processor.processLargeDataset([1, 2, 3]); // ‚è±Ô∏è Logs execution time

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Method decorator receives target, propertyName, descriptor
```

**3. Property Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ PROPERTY DECORATOR for validation
function required(target: any, propertyName: string) {
  // Store metadata v·ªÅ required fields
  const requiredFields = Reflect.getMetadata('required', target) || [];
  requiredFields.push(propertyName);
  Reflect.defineMetadata('required', requiredFields, target);
}

function validate(target: any) {
  const requiredFields: string[] = Reflect.getMetadata('required', target) || [];

  for (const field of requiredFields) {
    if (!target[field]) {
      throw new Error(`Field ${field} is required`);
    }
  }
}

class User {
  @required
  name: string;

  @required
  email: string;

  age?: number;

  constructor(name: string, email: string, age?: number) {
    this.name = name;
    this.email = email;
    this.age = age;

    validate(this); // ‚úÖ Validate required fields
  }
}

// Usage
const user1 = new User("John", "john@email.com"); // ‚úÖ OK
// const user2 = new User("", "john@email.com"); // ‚ùå Error: Field name is required

// üìù GHI NH·ªû: Property decorator receives target v√† propertyName
```

**4. Parameter Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ PARAMETER DECORATOR for dependency injection
function inject(token: string) {
  return function (target: any, propertyName: string | symbol, parameterIndex: number) {
    // Store injection metadata
    const existingTokens = Reflect.getMetadata('inject', target) || [];
    existingTokens[parameterIndex] = token;
    Reflect.defineMetadata('inject', existingTokens, target);
  };
}

// Simple DI Container
class Container {
  private services = new Map<string, any>();

  register(token: string, service: any) {
    this.services.set(token, service);
  }

  resolve<T>(constructor: new (...args: any[]) => T): T {
    const tokens: string[] = Reflect.getMetadata('inject', constructor) || [];
    const dependencies = tokens.map(token => this.services.get(token));
    return new constructor(...dependencies);
  }
}

// Services
class Logger {
  log(message: string) {
    console.log(`[LOG]: ${message}`);
  }
}

class Database {
  query(sql: string) {
    console.log(`Executing: ${sql}`);
  }
}

// Service with dependencies
class UserService {
  constructor(
    @inject('logger') private logger: Logger,
    @inject('database') private database: Database
  ) {}

  getUser(id: number) {
    this.logger.log(`Getting user ${id}`);
    this.database.query(`SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ${id}`);
  }
}

// Usage
const container = new Container();
container.register('logger', new Logger());
container.register('database', new Database());

const userService = container.resolve(UserService);
userService.getUser(1);

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Parameter decorator receives target, propertyName, parameterIndex
```

#### **‚ö° ADVANCED PATTERNS:**

**1. Decorator Factory Pattern:**
```typescript
// üéØ DECORATOR FACTORY - Function that returns decorator
function cache(ttl: number = 5000) {
  const cacheStore = new Map<string, { data: any; timestamp: number }>();

  return function (target: any, propertyName: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
    const originalMethod = descriptor.value;

    descriptor.value = function (...args: any[]) {
      const key = `${propertyName}_${JSON.stringify(args)}`;
      const cached = cacheStore.get(key);

      // ‚úÖ Return cached result if valid
      if (cached && (Date.now() - cached.timestamp) < ttl) {
        console.log(`Cache hit for ${propertyName}`);
        return cached.data;
      }

      // ‚úÖ Execute v√† cache result
      const result = originalMethod.apply(this, args);
      cacheStore.set(key, { data: result, timestamp: Date.now() });
      console.log(`Cache miss for ${propertyName}`);
      return result;
    };
  };
}

class ApiService {
  @cache(3000) // Cache for 3 seconds
  fetchUser(id: number) {
    console.log(`Fetching user ${id} from API...`);
    return { id, name: `User ${id}` };
  }
}

// Test caching
const api = new ApiService();
api.fetchUser(1); // Cache miss
api.fetchUser(1); // Cache hit (within 3s)
```

**2. Multiple Decorators (Composition):**
```typescript
// üéØ MULTIPLE DECORATORS - Applied bottom to top
function log(target: any, propertyName: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
  const method = descriptor.value;
  descriptor.value = function (...args: any[]) {
    console.log(`Calling ${propertyName} with args:`, args);
    return method.apply(this, args);
  };
}

function retry(attempts: number = 3) {
  return function (target: any, propertyName: string, descriptor: PropertyDescriptor) {
    const method = descriptor.value;

    descriptor.value = async function (...args: any[]) {
      for (let i = 0; i < attempts; i++) {
        try {
          return await method.apply(this, args);
        } catch (error) {
          console.log(`Attempt ${i + 1} failed:`, error);
          if (i === attempts - 1) throw error;
        }
      }
    };
  };
}

class NetworkService {
  @log           // ‚úÖ Applied second (outer)
  @retry(3)      // ‚úÖ Applied first (inner)
  async fetchData(url: string) {
    // Simulate random failure
    if (Math.random() > 0.7) {
      throw new Error('Network error');
    }
    return `Data from ${url}`;
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Decorators execute BOTTOM to TOP (nh∆∞ function composition)
```

#### **üéØ REAL-WORLD EXAMPLES:**

**1. Angular-style Component Decorator:**
```typescript
interface ComponentConfig {
  selector: string;
  template: string;
  styles?: string[];
}

// üéØ COMPONENT FRAMEWORK v·ªõi decorators
function Component(config: ComponentConfig) {
  return function <T extends { new(...args: any[]): {} }>(constructor: T) {
    // Add metadata to class
    Reflect.defineMetadata('component', config, constructor);

    return class extends constructor {
      // ‚úÖ Add framework functionality
      private _selector = config.selector;
      private _template = config.template;

      render(container: HTMLElement) {
        container.innerHTML = this._template;
        console.log(`Component ${this._selector} rendered`);
      }
    };
  };
}

@Component({
  selector: 'user-profile',
  template: '<div class="user">{{name}}</div>',
  styles: ['div.user { color: blue; }']
})
class UserProfileComponent {
  name: string = 'John Doe';
}
```

**2. Express-style Route Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ EXPRESS ROUTING v·ªõi decorators
const routes: Array<{
  method: string;
  path: string;
  handler: string;
  target: any;
}> = [];

function Get(path: string) {
  return function (target: any, propertyName: string) {
    routes.push({
      method: 'GET',
      path,
      handler: propertyName,
      target: target.constructor
    });
  };
}

function Post(path: string) {
  return function (target: any, propertyName: string) {
    routes.push({
      method: 'POST',
      path,
      handler: propertyName,
      target: target.constructor
    });
  };
}

class UserController {
  @Get('/users')
  getUsers() {
    return [{ id: 1, name: 'John' }];
  }

  @Post('/users')
  createUser() {
    return { id: 2, name: 'Jane' };
  }

  @Get('/users/:id')
  getUser() {
    return { id: 1, name: 'John' };
  }
}

// Framework integration
function createRouter() {
  console.log('Registered routes:');
  routes.forEach(route => {
    console.log(`${route.method} ${route.path} -> ${route.target.name}.${route.handler}`);
  });
}

createRouter();
// Output:
// GET /users -> UserController.getUsers
// POST /users -> UserController.createUser
// GET /users/:id -> UserController.getUser
```

**3. Validation Decorators:**
```typescript
// üéØ VALIDATION DECORATORS
function IsEmail(target: any, propertyName: string) {
  addValidator(target, propertyName, (value: string) => {
    const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
    return emailRegex.test(value) || `${propertyName} must be a valid email`;
  });
}

function MinLength(length: number) {
  return function (target: any, propertyName: string) {
    addValidator(target, propertyName, (value: string) => {
      return value.length >= length || `${propertyName} must be at least ${length} characters`;
    });
  };
}

function addValidator(target: any, propertyName: string, validator: (value: any) => boolean | string) {
  const validators = Reflect.getMetadata('validators', target) || {};
  validators[propertyName] = validators[propertyName] || [];
  validators[propertyName].push(validator);
  Reflect.defineMetadata('validators', validators, target);
}

function validate(obj: any): string[] {
  const validators = Reflect.getMetadata('validators', obj) || {};
  const errors: string[] = [];

  for (const [property, validatorList] of Object.entries(validators)) {
    const value = obj[property];
    for (const validator of validatorList as Function[]) {
      const result = validator(value);
      if (result !== true) {
        errors.push(result);
      }
    }
  }

  return errors;
}

class RegisterDto {
  @IsEmail
  email: string;

  @MinLength(8)
  password: string;

  constructor(email: string, password: string) {
    this.email = email;
    this.password = password;
  }
}

// Usage
const dto1 = new RegisterDto("test@email.com", "password123");
console.log(validate(dto1)); // []

const dto2 = new RegisterDto("invalid-email", "123");
console.log(validate(dto2)); // ["email must be a valid email", "password must be at least 8 characters"]
```

#### **üí° INTERVIEW INSIGHTS:**

**üîπ DECORATOR EXECUTION ORDER:**
```typescript
@first
@second
@third
class MyClass {}

// Execution: third() ‚Üí second() ‚Üí first()
// Like: first(second(third(MyClass)))
```

**üîπ PERFORMANCE CONSIDERATIONS:**
- Decorators run at **CLASS DEFINITION TIME**, not instantiation
- **NO RUNTIME OVERHEAD** for simple decorators
- **METADATA STORAGE** can increase memory usage
- **METHOD WRAPPING** c√≥ th·ªÉ affect performance

**üîπ BROWSER SUPPORT:**
- C·∫ßn **POLYFILL** cho `reflect-metadata`
- **BABEL/TSC** transforms decorators to regular JavaScript
- Modern frameworks handle n√†y automatically

**üîπ ALTERNATIVES TO DECORATORS:**
```typescript
// Instead of decorators, you can use:

// 1. Higher-Order Functions
const withLogging = (fn: Function) => (...args: any[]) => {
  console.log('Calling function');
  return fn(...args);
};

// 2. Class Mixins
function LoggingMixin<T extends Constructor>(Base: T) {
  return class extends Base {
    log(message: string) {
      console.log(message);
    }
  };
}

// 3. Composition Pattern
class Logger {
  static wrap(method: Function) {
    return (...args: any[]) => {
      console.log('Method called');
      return method(...args);
    };
  }
}
```

#### **üöÄ BEST PRACTICES:**

**üìù DO's:**
- ‚úÖ Use for **CROSS-CUTTING CONCERNS** (logging, caching, validation)
- ‚úÖ Keep decorators **SIMPLE v√† FOCUSED**
- ‚úÖ **DOCUMENT** decorator behavior clearly
- ‚úÖ Consider **COMPOSITION** over complex inheritance

**üìù DON'Ts:**
- ‚ùå Don't use for **BUSINESS LOGIC**
- ‚ùå Avoid **DEEPLY NESTED** decorator logic
- ‚ùå Don't **OVERUSE** decorators (readability impact)
- ‚ùå Avoid **SIDE EFFECTS** in decorator factories

**GHI NH·ªö:** Decorators = **METADATA + BEHAVIOR MODIFICATION** at compile/definition time! Perfect for **FRAMEWORK DEVELOPMENT** v√† **ASPECT-ORIENTED PROGRAMMING**! üéØ

---

### TS8: Generics trong TypeScript - Concept v√† Examples?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

Generics l√† **POWERFUL FEATURE** cho ph√©p t·∫°o **REUSABLE COMPONENTS** v·ªõi **FLEXIBLE TYPES**. Thay v√¨ hardcode specific types, generics cho ph√©p **PARAMETERIZE TYPES**!

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL CONCEPT:**

**Generics = PLACEHOLDER for TYPES**

```typescript
// ‚ùå WITHOUT GENERICS: Type-specific functions
function getStringArray(): string[] {
  return [];
}

function getNumberArray(): number[] {
  return [];
}

function getBooleanArray(): boolean[] {
  return [];
}

// ‚úÖ WITH GENERICS: One function, any type!
function getArray<T>(): T[] {
  return [];
}

// Usage - TypeScript infers the type
const strings = getArray<string>(); // string[]
const numbers = getArray<number>(); // number[]
const booleans = getArray<boolean>(); // boolean[]

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: T = Type Parameter (c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒë·∫∑t t√™n g√¨ c≈©ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c: K, V, U, etc.)
```

#### **üõ†Ô∏è BASIC GENERIC SYNTAX:**

**1. Function Generics:**
```typescript
// üéØ GENERIC FUNCTION v·ªõi type parameter T
function identity<T>(arg: T): T {
  return arg; // Input type = Output type
}

// ‚úÖ USAGE - Explicit type
const result1 = identity<string>("hello"); // result1: string
const result2 = identity<number>(42); // result2: number

// ‚úÖ USAGE - Type inference (TypeScript t·ª± ƒëo√°n)
const result3 = identity("hello"); // result3: string (inferred)
const result4 = identity(42); // result4: number (inferred)

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Type inference makes generics MORE CONVENIENT!
```

**2. Generic Arrays:**
```typescript
// üéØ WORKING WITH GENERIC ARRAYS
function getFirstElement<T>(array: T[]): T | undefined {
  return array.length > 0 ? array[0] : undefined;
}

// Usage
const firstString = getFirstElement(["a", "b", "c"]); // string | undefined
const firstNumber = getFirstElement([1, 2, 3]); // number | undefined
const firstUser = getFirstElement([
  { id: 1, name: "John" },
  { id: 2, name: "Jane" }
]); // { id: number; name: string; } | undefined

// üéØ GENERIC ARRAY OPERATIONS
function reverseArray<T>(array: T[]): T[] {
  return array.slice().reverse(); // ‚úÖ Preserve original array
}

const reversedStrings = reverseArray(["a", "b", "c"]); // string[]
const reversedNumbers = reverseArray([1, 2, 3]); // number[]
```

#### **üèóÔ∏è GENERIC CLASSES:**

```typescript
// üéØ GENERIC CLASS for data storage
class Container<T> {
  private items: T[] = [];

  add(item: T): void {
    this.items.push(item);
  }

  get(index: number): T | undefined {
    return this.items[index];
  }

  getAll(): T[] {
    return [...this.items]; // ‚úÖ Return copy
  }

  size(): number {
    return this.items.length;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Generic method within generic class
  filter(predicate: (item: T) => boolean): T[] {
    return this.items.filter(predicate);
  }
}

// Usage
const stringContainer = new Container<string>();
stringContainer.add("hello");
stringContainer.add("world");
console.log(stringContainer.getAll()); // ["hello", "world"]

const numberContainer = new Container<number>();
numberContainer.add(1);
numberContainer.add(2);
const evenNumbers = numberContainer.filter(n => n % 2 === 0); // number[]

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Generic classes create TYPE-SAFE containers!
```

#### **üîó GENERIC INTERFACES:**

```typescript
// üéØ GENERIC INTERFACE ƒë·ªãnh nghƒ©a contract
interface Repository<T> {
  save(entity: T): T;
  findById(id: string): T | null;
  findAll(): T[];
  delete(id: string): boolean;
}

// ‚úÖ IMPLEMENTATION cho specific type
interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

class UserRepository implements Repository<User> {
  private users: User[] = [];

  save(user: User): User {
    const existingIndex = this.users.findIndex(u => u.id === user.id);
    if (existingIndex >= 0) {
      this.users[existingIndex] = user; // Update
    } else {
      this.users.push(user); // Create
    }
    return user;
  }

  findById(id: string): User | null {
    return this.users.find(u => u.id === id) || null;
  }

  findAll(): User[] {
    return [...this.users];
  }

  delete(id: string): boolean {
    const index = this.users.findIndex(u => u.id === id);
    if (index >= 0) {
      this.users.splice(index, 1);
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  }
}

// Usage
const userRepo = new UserRepository();
const user = userRepo.save({ id: "1", name: "John", email: "john@email.com" });
```

#### **‚ö° ADVANCED GENERIC PATTERNS:**

**1. Multiple Type Parameters:**
```typescript
// üéØ MULTIPLE GENERICS for key-value pairs
class KeyValueStore<K, V> {
  private items = new Map<K, V>();

  set(key: K, value: V): void {
    this.items.set(key, value);
  }

  get(key: K): V | undefined {
    return this.items.get(key);
  }

  has(key: K): boolean {
    return this.items.has(key);
  }

  entries(): [K, V][] {
    return Array.from(this.items.entries());
  }
}

// Usage
const stringToNumberStore = new KeyValueStore<string, number>();
stringToNumberStore.set("age", 25);
stringToNumberStore.set("height", 175);

const userToPermissionStore = new KeyValueStore<User, string[]>();
userToPermissionStore.set(user, ["read", "write"]);

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Use multiple type parameters for RELATED but DIFFERENT types!
```

**2. Generic Constraints:**
```typescript
// üéØ CONSTRAINTS limit generic types
interface Lengthwise {
  length: number;
}

// ‚úÖ T must have length property
function logLength<T extends Lengthwise>(arg: T): T {
  console.log(`Length: ${arg.length}`);
  return arg;
}

// Usage
logLength("hello"); // ‚úÖ string has length
logLength([1, 2, 3]); // ‚úÖ array has length
logLength({ length: 10, value: "test" }); // ‚úÖ object with length

// logLength(123); // ‚ùå Error: number doesn't have length

// üéØ CONSTRAINT with keyof
function getProperty<T, K extends keyof T>(obj: T, key: K): T[K] {
  return obj[key]; // ‚úÖ Type-safe property access
}

// Usage
const person = { name: "John", age: 30, email: "john@email.com" };
const name = getProperty(person, "name"); // string
const age = getProperty(person, "age"); // number
// const invalid = getProperty(person, "salary"); // ‚ùå Error: salary doesn't exist

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Constraints ensure generics meet MINIMUM REQUIREMENTS!
```

**3. Conditional Types:**
```typescript
// üéØ CONDITIONAL TYPES v·ªõi generics
type ApiResponse<T> = T extends string
  ? { message: T }
  : T extends number
    ? { count: T }
    : { data: T };

// Usage
type StringResponse = ApiResponse<string>; // { message: string }
type NumberResponse = ApiResponse<number>; // { count: number }
type UserResponse = ApiResponse<User>; // { data: User }

// üéØ UTILITY TYPE v·ªõi conditional generics
type NonNullable<T> = T extends null | undefined ? never : T;

type SafeString = NonNullable<string | null>; // string
type SafeNumber = NonNullable<number | undefined>; // number
```

#### **üéØ REAL-WORLD EXAMPLES:**

**1. Generic API Client:**
```typescript
// üéØ TYPE-SAFE API CLIENT
interface ApiResponse<T> {
  data: T;
  status: number;
  message: string;
}

class ApiClient {
  private baseUrl: string;

  constructor(baseUrl: string) {
    this.baseUrl = baseUrl;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Generic GET method
  async get<T>(endpoint: string): Promise<ApiResponse<T>> {
    const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`);
    const data = await response.json();

    return {
      data: data as T, // Type assertion (in real app, add validation)
      status: response.status,
      message: response.statusText
    };
  }

  // ‚úÖ Generic POST method
  async post<TRequest, TResponse>(
    endpoint: string,
    body: TRequest
  ): Promise<ApiResponse<TResponse>> {
    const response = await fetch(`${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify(body)
    });

    const data = await response.json();
    return {
      data: data as TResponse,
      status: response.status,
      message: response.statusText
    };
  }
}

// Usage
const apiClient = new ApiClient('https://api.example.com');

// ‚úÖ Type-safe API calls
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

interface CreateUserRequest {
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

// GET request
const usersResponse = await apiClient.get<User[]>('/users');
const users: User[] = usersResponse.data; // ‚úÖ Typed as User[]

// POST request
const newUserResponse = await apiClient.post<CreateUserRequest, User>(
  '/users',
  { name: 'John', email: 'john@email.com' }
);
const newUser: User = newUserResponse.data; // ‚úÖ Typed as User
```

**2. Generic Event Emitter:**
```typescript
// üéØ TYPE-SAFE EVENT EMITTER
type EventMap = Record<string, any>;

class TypedEventEmitter<T extends EventMap> {
  private listeners: {
    [K in keyof T]?: Array<(data: T[K]) => void>;
  } = {};

  // ‚úÖ Type-safe event registration
  on<K extends keyof T>(event: K, listener: (data: T[K]) => void): void {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) {
      this.listeners[event] = [];
    }
    this.listeners[event]!.push(listener);
  }

  // ‚úÖ Type-safe event emission
  emit<K extends keyof T>(event: K, data: T[K]): void {
    const eventListeners = this.listeners[event];
    if (eventListeners) {
      eventListeners.forEach(listener => listener(data));
    }
  }

  // ‚úÖ Remove listener
  off<K extends keyof T>(event: K, listener: (data: T[K]) => void): void {
    const eventListeners = this.listeners[event];
    if (eventListeners) {
      const index = eventListeners.indexOf(listener);
      if (index >= 0) {
        eventListeners.splice(index, 1);
      }
    }
  }
}

// Define event types
interface UserEvents {
  'user:created': { id: number; name: string };
  'user:updated': { id: number; changes: Partial<User> };
  'user:deleted': { id: number };
}

// Usage
const userEventEmitter = new TypedEventEmitter<UserEvents>();

// ‚úÖ Type-safe listeners
userEventEmitter.on('user:created', (data) => {
  console.log(`User created: ${data.name} (${data.id})`); // ‚úÖ data is typed
});

userEventEmitter.on('user:updated', (data) => {
  console.log(`User ${data.id} updated:`, data.changes); // ‚úÖ data is typed
});

// ‚úÖ Type-safe emission
userEventEmitter.emit('user:created', { id: 1, name: 'John' }); // ‚úÖ Correct type
// userEventEmitter.emit('user:created', { name: 'John' }); // ‚ùå Error: missing id

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: Generic EventEmitter provides COMPILE-TIME safety for events!
```

**3. Generic State Management:**
```typescript
// üéØ SIMPLE GENERIC STATE STORE
class Store<T> {
  private state: T;
  private listeners: Array<(state: T) => void> = [];

  constructor(initialState: T) {
    this.state = initialState;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Get current state
  getState(): T {
    return this.state;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Update state v·ªõi type safety
  setState(updater: (currentState: T) => T): void {
    this.state = updater(this.state);
    this.notifyListeners();
  }

  // ‚úÖ Subscribe to state changes
  subscribe(listener: (state: T) => void): () => void {
    this.listeners.push(listener);

    // Return unsubscribe function
    return () => {
      const index = this.listeners.indexOf(listener);
      if (index >= 0) {
        this.listeners.splice(index, 1);
      }
    };
  }

  private notifyListeners(): void {
    this.listeners.forEach(listener => listener(this.state));
  }
}

// Define app state type
interface AppState {
  user: User | null;
  theme: 'light' | 'dark';
  notifications: string[];
}

// Usage
const appStore = new Store<AppState>({
  user: null,
  theme: 'light',
  notifications: []
});

// ‚úÖ Type-safe state updates
appStore.setState(state => ({
  ...state,
  user: { id: 1, name: 'John', email: 'john@email.com' }
}));

appStore.setState(state => ({
  ...state,
  theme: 'dark' // ‚úÖ TypeScript ensures valid theme values
}));

// ‚úÖ Type-safe subscriptions
const unsubscribe = appStore.subscribe(state => {
  console.log('Current user:', state.user?.name); // ‚úÖ Optional chaining
  console.log('Theme:', state.theme); // ‚úÖ Typed as 'light' | 'dark'
});

// Cleanup
unsubscribe();
```

#### **üí° INTERVIEW INSIGHTS:**

**üîπ WHY USE GENERICS:**
- ‚úÖ **TYPE SAFETY** without sacrificing flexibility
- ‚úÖ **CODE REUSE** across different types
- ‚úÖ **BETTER IntelliSense** v√† autocomplete
- ‚úÖ **COMPILE-TIME ERROR DETECTION**
- ‚úÖ **SELF-DOCUMENTING CODE**

**üîπ GENERIC NAMING CONVENTIONS:**
```typescript
// Common conventions:
T = Type (most common)
K = Key
V = Value
U = Second type
E = Element
R = Return type
P = Props (React context)

// Examples:
Map<K, V>        // Key-Value mapping
Array<T>         // Array of Type T
Promise<T>       // Promise resolving to Type T
Record<K, V>     // Record with Key K and Value V
```

**üîπ PERFORMANCE:**
- Generics = **COMPILE TIME** feature only
- **NO RUNTIME OVERHEAD** - types are erased
- **Better OPTIMIZATION** due to type information

**üîπ COMMON MISTAKES:**
```typescript
// ‚ùå OVER-CONSTRAINING
function processItem<T extends object>(item: T): T {
  // What if T could be primitive?
}

// ‚úÖ BETTER
function processItem<T>(item: T): T {
  // More flexible
}

// ‚ùå UNNECESSARY GENERICS
function addNumbers<T extends number>(a: T, b: T): T {
  return (a + b) as T; // Type assertion needed - red flag!
}

// ‚úÖ BETTER
function addNumbers(a: number, b: number): number {
  return a + b; // Simple v√† clear
}
```

#### **üöÄ BEST PRACTICES:**

**üìù DO's:**
- ‚úÖ Use **MEANINGFUL NAMES** cho type parameters
- ‚úÖ Add **CONSTRAINTS** when needed
- ‚úÖ **LEVERAGE TYPE INFERENCE** when possible
- ‚úÖ Use generics for **REUSABLE COMPONENTS**

**üìù DON'Ts:**
- ‚ùå Don't **OVER-ENGINEER** v·ªõi unnecessary generics
- ‚ùå Avoid **TOO MANY** type parameters (max 3-4)
- ‚ùå Don't use generics just for **TYPE ASSERTION**
- ‚ùå Avoid **COMPLEX CONDITIONAL TYPES** without good reason

**GHI NH·ªû:** Generics = **FLEXIBLE TYPES** that maintain **TYPE SAFETY**! Perfect for building **REUSABLE v√† TYPE-SAFE** libraries v√† frameworks! üéØ

---

### TS9: Static Typing, `typeof`, `keyof` - Advanced Type Operations?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

ƒê√¢y l√† **ADVANCED TYPE OPERATIONS** trong TypeScript gi√∫p b·∫°n t·∫°o **DYNAMIC TYPES** v√† **TYPE-SAFE CODE** t·ª´ existing types v√† values. ƒê√¢y l√† **NEXT LEVEL** type manipulation!

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL CONCEPTS:**

**Static Typing + Runtime Reflection = POWERFUL TYPE SYSTEM**

```typescript
// üéØ STATIC TYPING: Types known at compile time
const user = {
  id: 1,
  name: "John",
  email: "john@email.com",
  age: 30
};

// ‚úÖ TypeScript KNOWS the exact shape
type UserType = typeof user;
// Equivalent to: { id: number; name: string; email: string; age: number; }

type UserKeys = keyof typeof user;
// Equivalent to: "id" | "name" | "email" | "age"

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: typeof = value to type, keyof = type to union of keys
```

#### **üõ†Ô∏è `typeof` OPERATOR:**

**1. Basic typeof Usage:**
```typescript
// üéØ EXTRACT TYPE from values
const config = {
  apiUrl: "https://api.example.com",
  timeout: 5000,
  retries: 3,
  enableLogging: true
} as const; // ‚úÖ as const for literal types

// ‚úÖ Extract type from value
type Config = typeof config;
// Result: {
//   readonly apiUrl: "https://api.example.com";
//   readonly timeout: 5000;
//   readonly retries: 3;
//   readonly enableLogging: true;
// }

// üéØ FUNCTION TYPE extraction
function calculateTotal(price: number, tax: number): number {
  return price + (price * tax);
}

type CalculateFunction = typeof calculateTotal;
// Result: (price: number, tax: number) => number

// ‚úÖ Use extracted function type
const myCalculator: CalculateFunction = (p, t) => p * (1 + t);
```

**2. Advanced typeof Patterns:**
```typescript
// üéØ COMPLEX OBJECT TYPES
const apiEndpoints = {
  users: {
    list: "/api/users",
    create: "/api/users",
    update: (id: number) => `/api/users/${id}`,
    delete: (id: number) => `/api/users/${id}`
  },
  posts: {
    list: "/api/posts",
    byUser: (userId: number) => `/api/posts?user=${userId}`
  }
} as const;

type ApiEndpoints = typeof apiEndpoints;
// Result: {
//   readonly users: {
//     readonly list: "/api/users";
//     readonly create: "/api/users";
//     readonly update: (id: number) => string;
//     readonly delete: (id: number) => string;
//   };
//   readonly posts: {
//     readonly list: "/api/posts";
//     readonly byUser: (userId: number) => string;
//   };
// }

// ‚úÖ Extract specific nested types
type UserEndpoints = typeof apiEndpoints.users;
type UpdateFunction = typeof apiEndpoints.users.update;

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: typeof preserves function signatures v√† nested structures
```

#### **üîë `keyof` OPERATOR:**

**1. Basic keyof Usage:**
```typescript
// üéØ EXTRACT KEYS as union type
interface User {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  createdAt: Date;
}

type UserKeys = keyof User;
// Result: "id" | "name" | "email" | "createdAt"

// ‚úÖ Type-safe property access
function getUserProperty<K extends keyof User>(user: User, key: K): User[K] {
  return user[key]; // ‚úÖ TypeScript knows exact return type
}

const user: User = {
  id: 1,
  name: "John",
  email: "john@email.com",
  createdAt: new Date()
};

const userName = getUserProperty(user, "name"); // string
const userId = getUserProperty(user, "id"); // number
const userDate = getUserProperty(user, "createdAt"); // Date
// const invalid = getUserProperty(user, "invalid"); // ‚ùå Error

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: keyof creates LITERAL UNION TYPES from object keys
```

**2. Advanced keyof Patterns:**
```typescript
// üéØ CONDITIONAL KEYOF
type StringKeys<T> = {
  [K in keyof T]: T[K] extends string ? K : never;
}[keyof T];

type NumberKeys<T> = {
  [K in keyof T]: T[K] extends number ? K : never;
}[keyof T];

interface MixedData {
  id: number;
  name: string;
  age: number;
  email: string;
  isActive: boolean;
}

type StringProperties = StringKeys<MixedData>; // "name" | "email"
type NumberProperties = NumberKeys<MixedData>; // "id" | "age"

// ‚úÖ Type-safe getters with filtering
function getStringProperty<T, K extends StringKeys<T>>(
  obj: T,
  key: K
): T[K] {
  return obj[key];
}

const data: MixedData = {
  id: 1,
  name: "John",
  age: 30,
  email: "john@email.com",
  isActive: true
};

const name = getStringProperty(data, "name"); // ‚úÖ string
const email = getStringProperty(data, "email"); // ‚úÖ string
// const age = getStringProperty(data, "age"); // ‚ùå Error: age is number
```

#### **‚ö° ADVANCED COMBINATIONS:**

**1. Dynamic Object Creation:**
```typescript
// üéØ TYPE-SAFE OBJECT BUILDERS
const formSchema = {
  username: { type: "string", required: true, minLength: 3 },
  email: { type: "email", required: true },
  age: { type: "number", required: false, min: 0, max: 120 },
  password: { type: "password", required: true, minLength: 8 }
} as const;

type FormSchema = typeof formSchema;
type FormFields = keyof FormSchema;

// ‚úÖ Extract form data type from schema
type FormData = {
  [K in FormFields]: FormSchema[K]["required"] extends true
    ? string
    : string | undefined;
};

// Result: {
//   username: string;
//   email: string;
//   age: string | undefined;
//   password: string;
// }

// ‚úÖ Type-safe form validation
function validateField<K extends FormFields>(
  field: K,
  value: string
): { valid: boolean; error?: string } {
  const fieldSchema = formSchema[field];

  if (fieldSchema.required && !value) {
    return { valid: false, error: `${field} is required` };
  }

  if ("minLength" in fieldSchema && value.length < fieldSchema.minLength) {
    return { valid: false, error: `${field} must be at least ${fieldSchema.minLength} characters` };
  }

  return { valid: true };
}

// Usage
const usernameValidation = validateField("username", "jo");
// { valid: false, error: "username must be at least 3 characters" }
```

**2. API Response Mapping:**
```typescript
// üéØ TYPE-SAFE API RESPONSE HANDLING
const apiRoutes = {
  "/users": { method: "GET", response: [] as User[] },
  "/users/:id": { method: "GET", response: {} as User },
  "/posts": { method: "GET", response: [] as Post[] },
  "/auth/login": { method: "POST", response: {} as { token: string; user: User } }
} as const;

type ApiRoutes = typeof apiRoutes;
type ApiPaths = keyof ApiRoutes;

// ‚úÖ Extract response types from routes
type ApiResponseMap = {
  [K in ApiPaths]: ApiRoutes[K]["response"];
};

// Result: {
//   "/users": User[];
//   "/users/:id": User;
//   "/posts": Post[];
//   "/auth/login": { token: string; user: User };
// }

// ‚úÖ Type-safe API client
async function apiCall<P extends ApiPaths>(
  path: P
): Promise<ApiResponseMap[P]> {
  const route = apiRoutes[path];

  // Simulate API call
  const response = await fetch(path as string);
  const data = await response.json();

  return data as ApiResponseMap[P]; // ‚úÖ Correctly typed return
}

// Usage v·ªõi perfect type inference
const users = await apiCall("/users"); // User[]
const user = await apiCall("/users/:id"); // User
const loginResult = await apiCall("/auth/login"); // { token: string; user: User }
```

**3. State Management Type Safety:**
```typescript
// üéØ REDUX-STYLE TYPE-SAFE ACTIONS
const actionCreators = {
  setUser: (user: User) => ({ type: "SET_USER" as const, payload: user }),
  setLoading: (loading: boolean) => ({ type: "SET_LOADING" as const, payload: loading }),
  addPost: (post: Post) => ({ type: "ADD_POST" as const, payload: post }),
  removePost: (id: number) => ({ type: "REMOVE_POST" as const, payload: id })
};

type ActionCreators = typeof actionCreators;
type ActionCreatorKeys = keyof ActionCreators;

// ‚úÖ Extract all possible action types
type Actions = ReturnType<ActionCreators[ActionCreatorKeys]>;
// Result: Union of all action types

// ‚úÖ Type-safe reducer
function appReducer(state: AppState, action: Actions): AppState {
  switch (action.type) {
    case "SET_USER":
      return { ...state, user: action.payload }; // ‚úÖ payload is User
    case "SET_LOADING":
      return { ...state, loading: action.payload }; // ‚úÖ payload is boolean
    case "ADD_POST":
      return { ...state, posts: [...state.posts, action.payload] }; // ‚úÖ payload is Post
    case "REMOVE_POST":
      return {
        ...state,
        posts: state.posts.filter(p => p.id !== action.payload) // ‚úÖ payload is number
      };
    default:
      return state;
  }
}

// ‚úÖ Type-safe action dispatcher
function createDispatcher<K extends ActionCreatorKeys>(
  reducerDispatch: (action: Actions) => void
) {
  return {
    [K in ActionCreatorKeys]: (...args: Parameters<ActionCreators[K]>) => {
      const action = actionCreators[K](...args);
      reducerDispatch(action);
    }
  } as {
    [K in ActionCreatorKeys]: ActionCreators[K]
  };
}
```

#### **üéØ REAL-WORLD PATTERNS:**

**1. Configuration Management:**
```typescript
// üéØ ENVIRONMENT-AWARE CONFIG
const baseConfig = {
  app: {
    name: "MyApp",
    version: "1.0.0"
  },
  api: {
    baseUrl: "https://api.example.com",
    timeout: 5000
  },
  features: {
    darkMode: true,
    analytics: true,
    notifications: false
  }
} as const;

type BaseConfig = typeof baseConfig;
type ConfigPaths = keyof BaseConfig;
type FeatureFlags = keyof BaseConfig["features"];

// ‚úÖ Type-safe config updater
function updateConfig<
  TPath extends ConfigPaths,
  TKey extends keyof BaseConfig[TPath]
>(
  path: TPath,
  key: TKey,
  value: BaseConfig[TPath][TKey]
): void {
  (baseConfig[path] as any)[key] = value; // Type-safe update
}

// Usage
updateConfig("features", "darkMode", false); // ‚úÖ boolean expected
updateConfig("api", "timeout", 3000); // ‚úÖ number expected
// updateConfig("features", "darkMode", "invalid"); // ‚ùå Error: string not assignable to boolean

// ‚úÖ Feature flag checker
function isFeatureEnabled<T extends FeatureFlags>(feature: T): boolean {
  return baseConfig.features[feature];
}

if (isFeatureEnabled("analytics")) {
  // Analytics code
}
```

**2. Database Query Builder:**
```typescript
// üéØ TYPE-SAFE QUERY BUILDER
const tableSchemas = {
  users: {
    id: "number",
    name: "string",
    email: "string",
    createdAt: "date"
  },
  posts: {
    id: "number",
    title: "string",
    content: "string",
    authorId: "number",
    publishedAt: "date"
  }
} as const;

type TableSchemas = typeof tableSchemas;
type TableNames = keyof TableSchemas;

// ‚úÖ Type-safe column selector
function select<
  TTable extends TableNames,
  TColumns extends (keyof TableSchemas[TTable])[]
>(
  table: TTable,
  columns: TColumns
): Pick<TableSchemas[TTable], TColumns[number]> {
  // Query building logic here
  return {} as Pick<TableSchemas[TTable], TColumns[number]>;
}

// Usage v·ªõi perfect type inference
const userQuery = select("users", ["id", "name", "email"]);
// Type: Pick<{ id: "number"; name: "string"; email: "string"; createdAt: "date" }, "id" | "name" | "email">

const postQuery = select("posts", ["title", "publishedAt"]);
// Type: Pick<{ id: "number"; title: "string"; content: "string"; authorId: "number"; publishedAt: "date" }, "title" | "publishedAt">

// ‚úÖ Type-safe where clause builder
function where<
  TTable extends TableNames,
  TColumn extends keyof TableSchemas[TTable]
>(
  table: TTable,
  column: TColumn,
  value: TableSchemas[TTable][TColumn]
): void {
  // WHERE clause logic
}

// Usage
where("users", "id", 1); // ‚úÖ number expected
where("users", "name", "John"); // ‚úÖ string expected
// where("users", "id", "invalid"); // ‚ùå Error: string not assignable to number
```

#### **üí° INTERVIEW INSIGHTS:**

**üîπ STATIC TYPING BENEFITS:**
- ‚úÖ **COMPILE-TIME** error detection
- ‚úÖ **INTELLISENSE** v√† autocomplete
- ‚úÖ **REFACTORING SAFETY** - renaming variables/properties
- ‚úÖ **SELF-DOCUMENTING** code
- ‚úÖ **PERFORMANCE** - no runtime type checking needed

**üîπ TYPEOF vs KEYOF:**

| Operator | **Input** | **Output** | **Use Case** |
|----------|-----------|------------|-------------|
| `typeof` | **Value** | **Type** | Extract type from runtime value |
| `keyof` | **Type** | **Union of Keys** | Get property names as literal types |

**üîπ COMMON PATTERNS:**
```typescript
// Pattern 1: typeof + keyof combination
const obj = { a: 1, b: "hello" };
type ObjKeys = keyof typeof obj; // "a" | "b"

// Pattern 2: Generic type-safe property access
function getProp<T, K extends keyof T>(obj: T, key: K): T[K] {
  return obj[key];
}

// Pattern 3: Conditional type v·ªõi keyof
type StringKeys<T> = {
  [K in keyof T]: T[K] extends string ? K : never;
}[keyof T];
```

**üîπ PERFORMANCE:**
- **NO RUNTIME OVERHEAD** - all operations compile-time only
- **Better OPTIMIZATION** - TypeScript compiler can optimize better
- **TREE SHAKING** - unused properties can be eliminated

#### **üöÄ ADVANCED USE CASES:**

**1. Type-Safe Event System:**
```typescript
// üéØ EVENT SYSTEM v·ªõi static typing
const eventMap = {
  "user:login": (data: { userId: number; timestamp: Date }) => {},
  "user:logout": (data: { userId: number }) => {},
  "post:created": (data: { postId: number; authorId: number }) => {},
  "post:deleted": (data: { postId: number }) => {}
} as const;

type EventMap = typeof eventMap;
type EventNames = keyof EventMap;

class TypedEventEmitter {
  private listeners: {
    [K in EventNames]?: Array<Parameters<EventMap[K]>[0]>
  } = {};

  on<K extends EventNames>(
    event: K,
    callback: EventMap[K]
  ): void {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) {
      this.listeners[event] = [];
    }
    (this.listeners[event] as any[]).push(callback);
  }

  emit<K extends EventNames>(
    event: K,
    data: Parameters<EventMap[K]>[0]
  ): void {
    const callbacks = this.listeners[event];
    if (callbacks) {
      callbacks.forEach(callback => callback(data));
    }
  }
}

// Usage v·ªõi full type safety
const emitter = new TypedEventEmitter();

emitter.on("user:login", (data) => {
  console.log(`User ${data.userId} logged in at ${data.timestamp}`);
  // ‚úÖ data is correctly typed as { userId: number; timestamp: Date }
});

emitter.emit("user:login", { userId: 123, timestamp: new Date() }); // ‚úÖ Correct
// emitter.emit("user:login", { userId: "123" }); // ‚ùå Error: string not assignable to number
```

**2. Form Builder v·ªõi Type Safety:**
```typescript
// üéØ FORM BUILDER system
const formFields = {
  textInput: { type: "text", validation: (v: string) => v.length > 0 },
  emailInput: { type: "email", validation: (v: string) => /\S+@\S+\.\S+/.test(v) },
  numberInput: { type: "number", validation: (v: number) => !isNaN(v) },
  selectInput: {
    type: "select",
    options: ["option1", "option2", "option3"] as const,
    validation: (v: string) => v.length > 0
  }
} as const;

type FormFields = typeof formFields;
type FieldNames = keyof FormFields;

// ‚úÖ Dynamic form type generation
type FormSchema<T extends Record<string, FieldNames>> = {
  [K in keyof T]: T[K] extends FieldNames
    ? FormFields[T[K]] extends { type: "number" }
      ? number
      : FormFields[T[K]] extends { type: "select", options: readonly any[] }
        ? FormFields[T[K]]["options"][number]
        : string
    : never;
};

// Usage
const myFormConfig = {
  username: "textInput",
  email: "emailInput",
  age: "numberInput",
  country: "selectInput"
} as const;

type MyFormData = FormSchema<typeof myFormConfig>;
// Result: {
//   username: string;
//   email: string;
//   age: number;
//   country: "option1" | "option2" | "option3";
// }

// ‚úÖ Type-safe form validator
function validateForm<T extends Record<string, FieldNames>>(
  config: T,
  data: FormSchema<T>
): { valid: boolean; errors: Partial<Record<keyof T, string>> } {
  const errors: Partial<Record<keyof T, string>> = {};

  for (const [fieldName, fieldType] of Object.entries(config)) {
    const field = formFields[fieldType as FieldNames];
    const value = data[fieldName as keyof T];

    if (!field.validation(value as any)) {
      errors[fieldName as keyof T] = `Invalid ${fieldName}`;
    }
  }

  return {
    valid: Object.keys(errors).length === 0,
    errors
  };
}
```

#### **üéØ DECISION FRAMEWORK:**

```
‚ùì Need to extract type from existing value?
   ‚îî‚îÄ Use `typeof`

‚ùì Need to get keys of a type as union?
   ‚îî‚îÄ Use `keyof`

‚ùì Need both operations combined?
   ‚îî‚îÄ Use `keyof typeof value`

‚ùì Need conditional type based on properties?
   ‚îî‚îÄ Use mapped types v·ªõi `keyof`

‚ùì Need type-safe property access?
   ‚îî‚îÄ Use generics v·ªõi `keyof` constraint
```

**üìù GOLDEN RULES:**
1. **typeof** = convert runtime VALUES to compile-time TYPES
2. **keyof** = extract KEYS from types as literal unions
3. **Combine them** for maximum type safety
4. **Use generics** v·ªõi keyof constraints for reusable type-safe functions
5. **as const** ƒë·ªÉ preserve literal types when using typeof

**GHI NH·ªö:**
- `typeof value` = **VALUE ‚Üí TYPE**
- `keyof Type` = **TYPE ‚Üí KEY UNION**
- `keyof typeof value` = **VALUE ‚Üí KEY UNION**

**INTERVIEW TIP:** Demonstrate knowledge c·ªßa advanced type operations v√† how they enable **RUNTIME-SAFE** code v·ªõi **COMPILE-TIME** guarantees! üéØ

---

### TS10: OOP trong TypeScript - Abstract Class, Implement, Extend?

**Tr·∫£ l·ªùi:**

TypeScript mang **FULL OBJECT-ORIENTED PROGRAMMING** v√†o JavaScript v·ªõi **STRONG TYPING**! ƒê√¢y l√† **CORE CONCEPTS** m√† m·ªçi Senior Developer c·∫ßn n·∫Øm v·ªØng.

#### **üî• FUNDAMENTAL OOP CONCEPTS:**

**OOP in TypeScript = Classes + Inheritance + Polymorphism + Encapsulation + Abstraction**

```typescript
// üéØ BASIC CLASS STRUCTURE
class Animal {
  // ‚úÖ ENCAPSULATION: Private, Protected, Public
  private id: number;           // ‚ùå Ch·ªâ class n√†y access ƒë∆∞·ª£c
  protected name: string;       // ‚úÖ Class n√†y + subclasses
  public species: string;       // ‚úÖ M·ªçi n∆°i ƒë·ªÅu access ƒë∆∞·ª£c

  constructor(id: number, name: string, species: string) {
    this.id = id;
    this.name = name;
    this.species = species;
  }

  // ‚úÖ PUBLIC METHOD
  public makeSound(): string {
    return "Some generic animal sound";
  }

  // ‚úÖ PROTECTED METHOD (for subclasses)
  protected getName(): string {
    return this.name;
  }

  // ‚úÖ PRIVATE METHOD (internal only)
  private generateId(): number {
    return Math.random() * 1000;
  }
}

// üìù GHI NH·ªö:
// private = ch·ªâ class hi·ªán t·∫°i
// protected = class hi·ªán t·∫°i + subclasses
// public = m·ªçi n∆°i (default)
```

#### **üèóÔ∏è INHERITANCE v·ªõi EXTENDS:**

```typescript
// üéØ EXTENDS: Class inheritance
class Dog extends Animal {
  private breed: string;

  constructor(id: number, name: string, breed: string) {
    super(id, name, "Canine"); // ‚úÖ Call parent constructor
    this.breed = breed;
  }

  // ‚úÖ OVERRIDE parent method
  public makeSound(): string {
    return "Woof! Woof!";
  }

  // ‚úÖ ACCESS protected member t·ª´ parent
  public introduce(): string {
    return `I'm ${this.getName()}, a ${this.breed} dog`; // ‚úÖ getName() is protected
  }

  // ‚úÖ NEW method specific to Dog
  public fetch(item: string): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is fetching ${item}`;
  }

  // ‚úÖ GETTER/SETTER pattern
  get breedInfo(): string {
    return this.breed;
  }

  set breedInfo(newBreed: string) {
    if (newBreed.length > 0) {
      this.breed = newBreed;
    }
  }
}

// Usage
const myDog = new Dog(1, "Buddy", "Golden Retriever");
console.log(myDog.makeSound()); // "Woof! Woof!" (overridden)
console.log(myDog.introduce()); // "I'm Buddy, a Golden Retriever dog"
console.log(myDog.species); // "Canine" (public property)
// console.log(myDog.name); // ‚ùå Error: protected property
// console.log(myDog.id); // ‚ùå Error: private property

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: extends creates IS-A relationship (Dog IS AN Animal)
```

#### **üìã INTERFACES v·ªõi IMPLEMENTS:**

```typescript
// üéØ INTERFACES: Define contracts
interface Flyable {
  maxAltitude: number;
  fly(): string;
  land(): string;
}

interface Swimmable {
  maxDepth: number;
  swim(): string;
  dive(depth: number): string;
}

// ‚úÖ SINGLE INTERFACE implementation
class Bird extends Animal implements Flyable {
  maxAltitude: number;

  constructor(id: number, name: string, maxAltitude: number) {
    super(id, name, "Avian");
    this.maxAltitude = maxAltitude;
  }

  // ‚úÖ MUST implement interface methods
  fly(): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is flying up to ${this.maxAltitude}m`;
  }

  land(): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is landing safely`;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Override parent method
  makeSound(): string {
    return "Tweet! Tweet!";
  }
}

// ‚úÖ MULTIPLE INTERFACES implementation
class Duck extends Animal implements Flyable, Swimmable {
  maxAltitude: number;
  maxDepth: number;

  constructor(id: number, name: string) {
    super(id, name, "Waterfowl");
    this.maxAltitude = 100; // Ducks don't fly very high
    this.maxDepth = 5; // Shallow diving
  }

  // ‚úÖ Implement Flyable
  fly(): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is flying low over water`;
  }

  land(): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is landing on water`;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Implement Swimmable
  swim(): string {
    return `${this.getName()} is swimming gracefully`;
  }

  dive(depth: number): string {
    if (depth > this.maxDepth) {
      return `${this.getName()} can't dive that deep!`;
    }
    return `${this.getName()} is diving to ${depth}m`;
  }

  makeSound(): string {
    return "Quack! Quack!";
  }
}

// Usage
const eagle = new Bird(2, "Eagle", 3000);
console.log(eagle.fly()); // "Eagle is flying up to 3000m"

const duck = new Duck(3, "Donald");
console.log(duck.fly()); // "Donald is flying low over water"
console.log(duck.swim()); // "Donald is swimming gracefully"
console.log(duck.dive(3)); // "Donald is diving to 3m"

// üìù GHI NH·ªö: implements creates CAN-DO relationship (Duck CAN FLY and CAN SWIM)
```

#### **üèõÔ∏è ABSTRACT CLASSES:**

```typescript
// üéØ ABSTRACT CLASS: Cannot be instantiated directly
abstract class Vehicle {
  protected brand: string;
  protected model: string;
  protected year: number;

  constructor(brand: string, model: string, year: number) {
    this.brand = brand;
    this.model = model;
    this.year = year;
  }

  // ‚úÖ CONCRETE METHOD (c√≥ implementation)
  getInfo(): string {
    return `${this.year} ${this.brand} ${this.model}`;
  }

  // ‚úÖ ABSTRACT METHOD (must be implemented by subclasses)
  abstract start(): string;
  abstract stop(): string;
  abstract getMaxSpeed(): number;

  // ‚úÖ CONCRETE METHOD s·ª≠ d·ª•ng abstract method
  race(): string {
    const startMsg = this.start();
    const maxSpeed = this.getMaxSpeed();
    return `${startMsg} - Racing at max speed: ${maxSpeed} km/h`;
  }
}

// ‚úÖ CONCRETE implementation c·ªßa abstract class
class Car extends Vehicle {
  private engineType: string;

  constructor(brand: string, model: string, year: number, engineType: string) {
    super(brand, model, year);
    this.engineType = engineType;
  }

  // ‚úÖ MUST implement abstract methods
  start(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} engine started with ${this.engineType}`;
  }

  stop(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} engine stopped`;
  }

  getMaxSpeed(): number {
    return this.engineType === "electric" ? 200 : 180;
  }

  // ‚úÖ Additional car-specific methods
  openTrunk(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} trunk opened`;
  }
}

class Motorcycle extends Vehicle {
  private hasWindshield: boolean;

  constructor(brand: string, model: string, year: number, hasWindshield: boolean) {
    super(brand, model, year);
    this.hasWindshield = hasWindshield;
  }

  start(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} motorcycle engine roared to life`;
  }

  stop(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} motorcycle engine turned off`;
  }

  getMaxSpeed(): number {
    return this.hasWindshield ? 250 : 200; // Windshield allows higher speed
  }

  wheelie(): string {
    return `${this.getInfo()} doing a wheelie!`;
  }
}

// Usage
// const vehicle = new Vehicle("Generic", "Model", 2024); // ‚ùå Error: Cannot instantiate abstract class

const car = new Car("Tesla", "Model 3", 2024, "electric");
```
